<local-command-stdout>Version 0.2.21:  
• Fuzzy matching for /commands  

Version 0.2.26:  
• New /approved-tools command for managing tool permissions  
• Word-level diff display for improved code readability  
• Fuzzy matching for slash commands

• Added ANSI color theme for better terminal compatibility  
• Fixed issue where slash command arguments weren't being sent properly  
• (Mac-only) API keys are now stored in macOS Keychain  

Version 0.2.31:  
• Custom slash commands: Markdown files in .claude/commands/ directories now appear as custom slash commands to insert prompts into your conversation  
• MCP debug mode: Run with --mcp-debug flag to get more information about MCP server errors  

Version 0.2.32:  
• Interactive MCP setup wizard: Run "claude mcp add" to add MCP servers with a step-by-step interface  
• Fix for some PersistentShell issues  

Version 0.2.34:  
• Vim bindings for text input - enable with /vim or /config  

Version 0.2.36:  
• Import MCP servers from Claude Desktop with `claude mcp add-from-claude-desktop`  
• Add MCP servers as JSON strings with `claude mcp add-json <n> <json>`  

Version 0.2.37:  
• New /release-notes command lets you view release notes at any time  
• `claude config add/remove` commands now accept multiple values separated by commas or spaces  

Version 0.2.41:  
• MCP server startup timeout can now be configured via MCP_TIMEOUT environment variable  
• MCP server startup no longer blocks the app from starting up  

Version 0.2.44:  
• Ask Claude to make a plan with thinking mode: just say 'think' or 'think harder' or even 'ultrathink'  

Version 0.2.47:  
• Press Tab to auto-complete file and folder names  
• Press Shift + Tab to toggle auto-accept for file edits  
• Automatic conversation compaction for infinite conversation length (toggle with /config)  

Version 0.2.49:  
• Previous MCP server scopes have been renamed: previous "project" scope is now "local" and "global" scope is now "user"  

Version 0.2.50:  
• New MCP "project" scope now allows you to add MCP servers to .mcp.json files and commit them to your repository  

Version 0.2.53:  
• New web fetch tool lets Claude view URLs that you paste in  
• Fixed a bug with JPEG detection  

Version 0.2.54:  
• Quickly add to Memory by starting your message with '#'  
• Press ctrl+r to see full output for long tool results  
• Added support for MCP SSE transport  

Version 0.2.59:  
• Copy+paste images directly into your prompt  
• Improved progress indicators for bash and fetch tools  
• Bugfixes for non-interactive mode (-p)  

Version 0.2.61:  
• Navigate menus with vim-style keys (j/k) or bash/emacs shortcuts (Ctrl+n/p) for faster interaction  
• Enhanced image detection for more reliable clipboard paste functionality  
• Fixed an issue where ESC key could crash the conversation history selector  

Version 0.2.63:  
• Fixed an issue where MCP tools were loaded twice, which caused tool call errors  

Version 0.2.66:  
• Print mode (-p) now supports streaming output via --output-format=stream-json  
• Fixed issue where pasting coul

## <span style="color:#FFC107">◇ ASSISTANT</span>  *[2026-02-19 17:12:30]*

<details>
<summary>🔧 Tool: Read -- `team-acl.ts`</summary>

**Input:**

```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/team-acl.ts"
}
```

**Result:**

     1→/**  
     2→ * Team Resource ACL — checks whether an agent (or web UI request)  
     3→ * is allowed to access a given team's resources.  
     4→ *  
     5→ * Open teams (type undefined or 'open') impose no restrictions.  
     6→ * Closed teams restrict access to the manager, chief-of-staff,  
     7→ * and team members only.  
     8→ */  
     9→  
    10→import { isManager } from './governance'  
    11→import { getTeam } from './team-registry'  
    12→  
    13→export interface TeamAccessInput {  
    14→  teamId: string  
    15→  requestingAgentId?: string // undefined = web UI request (always allowed)  
    16→}  
    17→  
    18→export interface TeamAccessResult {  
    19→  allowed: boolean  
    20→  reason?: string  
    21→}  
    22→  
    23→/**  
    24→ * Determine whether the requester may access the team's resources.  
    25→ *  
    26→ * Decision order:  
    27→ *  1. Web UI (no agentId)      → allowed  
    28→ *  2. Team not found           → allowed (caller handles 404)  
    29→ *  3. Team is open / untyped   → allowed  
    30→ *  4. Requester is MANAGER     → allowed  
    31→ *  5. Requester is chief-of-staff → allowed  
    32→ *  6. Requester is a member    → allowed  
    33→ *  7. Otherwise                → denied  
    34→ */  
    35→export function checkTeamAccess(input: TeamAccessInput): TeamAccessResult {  
    36→  // 1. Web UI requests (no X-Agent-Id header) always pass  
    37→  if (input.requestingAgentId === undefined) {  
    38→    return { allowed: true }  
    39→  }  
    40→  
    41→  // 2. Team not found — let the caller deal with 404  
    42→  const team = getTeam(input.teamId)  
    43→  if (!team) {  
    44→    return { allowed: true }  
    45→  }  
    46→  
    47→  // 3. Open teams (or teams with no explicit type) have no ACL  
    48→  if (team.type !== 'closed') {  
    49→    return { allowed: true }  
    50→  }  
    51→  
    52→  // 4. MANAGER role always has access  
    53→  if (isManager(input.requestingAgentId)) {  
    54→    return { allowed: true }  
    55→  }  
    56→  
    57→  // 5.   

... [474 more chars truncated]  

</details>

<summary>🤖 Subagent (kraken): Fix team DELETE authorization SR-002</summary>

**Input:**

**Agent:** `kraken` | **Description:** Fix team DELETE authorization SR-002  

Fix 1 issue in `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/app/api/teams/[id]/route.ts`:  

**Issue SR-002**: The DELETE handler (starting at line 66) uses `checkTeamAccess()` for authorization. But `checkTeamAccess()` was designed for resource access (read/write) and allows ANY team member. This means any agent that is a member of a closed team can delete it, bypassing governance. Team deletion of a closed team should require MANAGER or Chief-of-Staff authority.  

**Fix**: After the existing `checkTeamAccess` check, add an additional authorization check for closed teams:  

1. The file already imports `getTeam` and `getManagerId` from the right places (line 2-3)  
2. Also import `isManager` from `@/lib/governance` — add it to the existing import from governance on line 3  
3. After the `checkTeamAccess` check (line 74-77), add:  
   ```typescript
   // SR-002 fix: Closed team deletion requires elevated authority (MANAGER or COS)
   // checkTeamAccess allows any member for resource access, but deletion is
... [963 more chars]

    16→  { params }: { params: Promise<{ id: string }> }  
    17→) {  
    18→  try {  
    19→    const { id } = await params  
    20→    const body = await request.json()  
    21→    const { action, resolvedBy, rejectReason } = body  
    22→  
    23→    if (!action || !resolvedBy) {  
    24→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'action and resolvedBy are required' }, { status: 400 })  
    25→    }  
    26→    if (action !== 'approve' && action !== 'reject') {  
    27→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'action must be "approve" or "reject"' }, { status: 400 })  
    28→    }  
    29→  
    30→    // Get the transfer request  
    31→    const transferReq = getTransferRequest(id)  
    32→    if (!transferReq) {  
    33→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Transfer request not found' }, { status: 404 })  
    34→    }  
    35→    if (transferReq.status !== 'pending') {  
    36→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Transfer request is already resolved' }, { status: 409 })  
    37→    }  
    38→  
    39→    // Acquire teams lock for the entire read-validate-write cycle to prevent TOCTOU races.  
    40→    // We use acquireLock directly (instead of withLock) because we need to return  
    41→    // NextResponse objects from within the critical section.  
    42→    const releaseLock  

... [5641 more chars truncated]

     2→ * Transfer Registry — manages team transfer requests  
     3→ *

    18→  
    19→function ensureDir(): void {  
    20→  if (!existsSync(AIMAESTRO_DIR)) {  
    21→    mkdirSync(AIMAESTRO_DIR, { recursive: true })  
    22→  }  
    23→}  
    24→  
    25→/** Load all transfer requests from disk */  
    26→export function loadTransfers(): TransferRequest[] {  
    27→  ensureDir()  
    28→  if (!existsSync(TRANSFERS_FILE)) {  
    29→    return []  
    30→  }  
    31→  try {  
    32→    const raw = readFileSync(TRANSFERS_FILE, 'utf-8')  
    33→    const data: TransfersFile = JSON.parse(raw)  
    34→    return data.requests || []  
    35→  } catch {  
    36→    return []  
    37→  }  
    38→}  
    39→  
    40→/** Save transfer requests to disk */  
    41→function saveTransfers(requests: TransferRequest[]): void {  
    42→  ensureDir()  
    43→  const data: TransfersFile = { version: 1, requests }  
    44→  writeFileSync(TRANSFERS_FILE, JSON.stringify(data, null, 2), 'utf-8')  
    45→}

## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-19 17:18:56]*

<div style="border-left: 4px solid #FF9800; padding-left: 12px; margin: 4px 0;">

Now I have a clear picture. Let me understand the issues:  

**SR-001**: The multi-closed-team constraint check (lines 86-101) runs AFTER `resolveTransferRequest()` (line 75) which marks the transfer as "approved" on disk. If the constraint fails, the transfer is "approved" but the agent was never moved.  

**SR-007**: If `saveTeams()` fails (line 126-129), the transfer is already "approved" on disk but the team mutation didn't happen.  

For SR-007, I see that `resolveTransferRequest` uses `withLock('transfers', ...)` and only accepts `'approved' | 'rejected'` as status. I need to create a way to revert. The simplest approach: use `loadTransfers` and `saveTransfers` directly, but `saveTransfers` is not exported. So I'll need to either export it or add a dedicated revert function to `transfer-registry.ts`.  

Let me now check the governance types to understand the TransferRequest type.

## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-19 17:20:11]*

<details>
<summary>🔧 Tool: Edit -- `transfer-registry.ts`</summary>

**Input:**

**File:** `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/transfer-registry.ts`  

**Old:**  
```
// Exported for future scheduled cleanup integration
/** Clean up old resolved requests (older than 30 days) */
```

**New:**  
```
/** Revert an approved/rejected transfer back to pending state.
 *  Used as a compensating action when a downstream operation (e.g. saveTeams)
 *  fails after the transfer was already marked as approved on disk. */
export async function revertTransferToPending(id: string): Promise<boolean> {
  return withLock('transfers', () => {
    const requests = loadTransfers()
    const idx = requests.findIndex(r => r.id === id)
    if (idx === -1) return false

    requests[idx] = {
      ...requests[idx],
      status: 'pending',
      resolvedAt: undefined,
      resolvedBy: undefined,
      rejectReason: undefined,
    }
    saveTransfers(requests)
    return true
  })
}

// Exported for future scheduled cleanup integration
/** Clean up old resolved requests (older than 30 days) */
```

**Result:**

The file /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/transfer-registry.ts has been updated successfully.  

</details>

## <span style="color:#2196F3">◆ USER</span>  *[2026-02-19 17:17:56]*

<div style="border-left: 4px solid #2196F3; padding-left: 12px; margin: 4px 0;">

Fix 3 issues across multiple files in `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/`:  

**Issue SR-003**: `bcrypt.hashSync`/`compareSync` in `lib/governance.ts` block the event loop (~300ms per call). Replace with async `bcrypt.hash`/`bcrypt.compare`.  

**Issue SR-004**: No rate limiting on governance password verification. Add an in-memory rate limiter.  

**Issue SR-011**: `loadGovernance()` catches ALL errors including JSON parse errors and returns defaults, silently masking disk corruption.  

## Changes Required:  

### 1. `lib/governance.ts` — 3 changes:  

**SR-003a**: Change `setPassword` to use async `bcrypt.hash`:  
```typescript
export async function setPassword(plaintext: string): Promise<void> {
  return withLock('governance', async () => {
    const config = loadGovernance()
    config.passwordHash = await bcrypt.hash(plaintext, BCRYPT_SALT_ROUNDS)
    config.passwordSetAt = new Date().toISOString()
    saveGovernance(config)
  })
}
```

**SR-003b**: Change `verifyPassword` to async with `bcrypt.compare`:  
```typescript
/** Verify plaintext against stored password hash. Returns false if no password set. */
export async function verifyPassword(plaintext: string): Promise<boolean> {
  const config = loadGovernance()
  if (!config.passwordHash) {
    // Phase 1 (localhost-only): timing difference between "no password" and "wrong password"
    // is accepted risk. No remote attackers can observe timing in this deployment model.
    return false
  }
  return bcrypt.compare(plaintext, config.passwordHash)
}
```

**SR-011**: Fix `loadGovernance` to distinguish file-not-found from parse errors:  
```typescript
export function loadGovernance(): GovernanceConfig {
  ensureAimaestroDir()
  if (!fs.existsSync(GOVERNANCE_FILE)) {
    // First-time initialization: write defaults and return them
    saveGovernance(DEFAULT_GOVERNANCE_CONFIG)
    return { ...DEFAULT_GOVERNANCE_CONFIG }
  }
  try {
    const data = fs.readFileSync(GOVERNANCE_FILE, 'utf-8')
    const parsed: GovernanceConfig = JSON.parse(data)
    return parsed
  } catch (error) {
    // Distinguish read errors from parse errors — parse errors indicate disk corruption
    if (error instanceof SyntaxError) {
      console.error('[governance] CORRUPTION: governance.json contains invalid JSON — returning defaults. Manual inspection required:', GOVERNANCE_FILE)
    } else {
      console.error('[governance] Failed to read governance config:', error)
    }
    return { ...DEFAULT_GOVERNANCE_CONFIG }
  }
}
```

     6→export async function POST(

     9→) {

    38→      const updated = await updateTeam(id, { chiefOfStaffId: null, type: 'open' }, managerId)  
    39→      return NextResponse.json({ success: true, team: updated })

## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-19 17:18:26]*

<details>
<summary>🔧 Tool: Read -- `file-lock.ts`</summary>

**Input:**

```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/file-lock.ts"
}
```

**Result:**

     1→/**  
     2→ * File Lock — in-process mutex for serializing load→modify→save operations  
     3→ *  
     4→ * Prevents concurrent read-modify-write races within a single Node.js process.  
     5→ * Each registry file gets its own named lock. When one API request is mid-write,  
     6→ * other requests for the same file queue up and run sequentially.  
     7→ *  
     8→ * This is sufficient for Phase 1 (single Next.js process, localhost).  
     9→ * For multi-process deployments, replace with advisory file locks (e.g., proper-lockfile).  
    10→ */  
    11→  
    12→// Map of lock name -> queue of pending resolve callbacks  
    13→const locks = new Map<string, Array<() => void>>()  
    14→// Set of currently held lock names  
    15→const held = new Set<string>()  
    16→  
    17→/**  
    18→ * Acquire a named lock. Returns a release function.  
    19→ * If the lock is already held, the caller awaits until it is released.  
    20→ */  
    21→export function acquireLock(name: string): Promise<() => void> {  
    22→  if (!held.has(name)) {  
    23→    // Lock is free — acquire immediately  
    24→    held.add(name)  
    25→    return Promise.resolve(() => releaseLock(name))  
    26→  }  
    27→  
    28→  // Lock is held — enqueue and wait  
    29→  return new Promise<() => void>((resolve) => {  
    30→    if (!locks.has(name)) {  
    31→      locks.set(name, [])  
    32→    }  
    33→    locks.get(name)!.push(() => {  
    34→      resolve(() => releaseLock(name))  
    35→    })  
    36→  })  
    37→}  
    38→  
    39→/**  
    40→ * Release a named lock and wake the next waiter if any.  
    41→ */  
    42→function releaseLock(name: string): void {  
    43→  const queue = locks.get(name)  
    44→  if (queue && queue.length > 0) {  
    45→    // Hand lock to next waiter (don't remove from held set)  
    46→    const next = queue.shift()!  
    47→    if (queue.length === 0) {  
    48→      locks.delete(name)  
    49→    }  
    50→    next()  
    51→  } else {  
    52→    // No waiters — release the lock  
    53→    hel  

... [473 more chars truncated]  

</details>

```
/** Load governance config from disk, creating with defaults if missing */
export function loadGovernance(): GovernanceConfig {
  try {
    ensureAimaestroDir()
    if (!fs.existsSync(GOVERNANCE_FILE)) {
      // First-time initialization: write defaults and return them
      saveGovernance(DEFAULT_GOVERNANCE_CONFIG)
      return { ...DEFAULT_GOVERNANCE_CONFIG }
    }
    const data = fs.readFileSync(GOVERNANCE_FILE, 'utf-8')
    const parsed: GovernanceConfig = JSON.parse(data)
    return parsed
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to load governance config:', error)
    return { ...DEFAULT_GOVERNANCE_CONFIG }
  }
}
```

**New:**  
```
/** Load governance config from disk, creating with defaults if missing */
export function loadGovernance(): GovernanceConfig {
  ensureAimaestroDir()
  if (!fs.existsSync(GOVERNANCE_FILE)) {
    // First-time initialization: write defaults and return them
    saveGovernance(DEFAULT_GOVERNANCE_CONFIG)
    return { ...DEFAULT_GOVERNANCE_CONFIG }
  }
  try {
    const data = fs.readFileSync(GOVERNANCE_FILE, 'utf-8')
    const parsed: GovernanceConfig = JSON.parse(data)
    return parsed
  } catch (error) {
    // Distinguish read errors from parse errors — parse errors indicate disk corruption
    if (error instanceof SyntaxError) {
      console.error('[governance] CORRUPTION: governance.json contains invalid JSON — returning defaults. Manual inspection required:', GOVERNANCE_FILE)
    } else {
      console.error('[governance] Failed to read governance config:', error)
    }
    return { ...DEFAULT_GOVERNANCE_CONFIG }
  }
}
```

**Result:**

The file /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/governance.ts has been updated successfully.  

</details>

/** Set governance password (bcrypt hash with 12 salt rounds) */
export async function setPassword(plaintext: string): Promise<void> {
  return withLock('governance', () => {
    const config = loadGovernance()
    config.passwordHash = bcrypt.hashSync(plaintext, BCRYPT_SALT_ROUNDS)
    config.passwordSetAt = new Date().toISOString()
    saveGovernance(config)
  })
}
```

**New:**  
```
/** Set governance password (bcrypt hash with 12 salt rounds) */
export async function setPassword(plaintext: string): Promise<void> {
  return withLock('governance', async () => {
    const config = loadGovernance()
    config.passwordHash = await bcrypt.hash(plaintext, BCRYPT_SALT_ROUNDS)
    config.passwordSetAt = new Date().toISOString()
    saveGovernance(config)
  })
}
```

**Result:**

The file /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/governance.ts has been updated successfully.

## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-19 17:18:50]*

<details>
<summary>🔧 Tool: Edit -- `governance.ts`</summary>

**Input:**

**Old:**  
```
/** Verify plaintext against stored password hash. Returns false if no password set. */
export function verifyPassword(plaintext: string): boolean {
  const config = loadGovernance()
  if (!config.passwordHash) {
    // Phase 1 (localhost-only): timing difference between "no password" and "wrong password"
    // is accepted risk. No remote attackers can observe timing in this deployment model.
    return false
  }
  return bcrypt.compareSync(plaintext, config.passwordHash)
}
```

**New:**  
```
/** Verify plaintext against stored password hash. Returns false if no password set. */
export async function verifyPassword(plaintext: string): Promise<boolean> {
  const config = loadGovernance()
  if (!config.passwordHash) {
    // Phase 1 (localhost-only): timing difference between "no password" and "wrong password"
    // is accepted risk. No remote attackers can observe timing in this deployment model.
    return false
  }
  return bcrypt.compare(plaintext, config.passwordHash)
}
```

The file /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/governance.ts has been updated successfully.

**New:**  
```
    // If password already set, require current password
    if (config.passwordHash) {
      // Rate limit password verification to prevent brute-force attacks
      const rateCheck = checkRateLimit('governance-password')
      if (!rateCheck.allowed) {
        return NextResponse.json(
          { error: `Too many failed password attempts. Try again in ${Math.ceil(rateCheck.retryAfterMs / 1000)}s` },
          { status: 429 }
        )
      }

      if (!currentPassword || !(await verifyPassword(currentPassword))) {
        recordFailure('governance-password')
        return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid current password' }, { status: 401 })
      }
      // Password verified successfully — reset rate limit counter
      resetRateLimit('governance-password')
    }
```

## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-19 17:19:49]*

<details>
<summary>🔧 Tool: Edit -- `governance.test.ts`</summary>

**Old:**  
```
describe('verifyPassword', () => {
  it('returns true for correct password and false for wrong password', () => {
    /** Verifies password comparison against stored hash returns correct boolean */
    seedGovernance({ passwordHash: 'hashed:correctpass' })

    expect(verifyPassword('correctpass')).toBe(true)
    expect(verifyPassword('wrongpass')).toBe(false)
  })

  it('returns false when no password has been set', () => {

    expect(verifyPassword('anypassword')).toBe(false)

**New:**  
```
describe('verifyPassword', () => {
  it('returns true for correct password and false for wrong password', async () => {
    /** Verifies password comparison against stored hash returns correct boolean */
    seedGovernance({ passwordHash: 'hashed:correctpass' })

    expect(await verifyPassword('correctpass')).toBe(true)
    expect(await verifyPassword('wrongpass')).toBe(false)
  })

  it('returns false when no password has been set', async () => {
    /** Verifies that verifyPassword returns false when passwordHash is null (no password configured) */
    seedGovernance({ passwordHash: null })

    expect(await verifyPassword('anypassword')).toBe(false)
  })
})
```

**Result:**

The file /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/tests/governance.test.ts has been updated successfully.

## <span style="color:#2196F3">◆ USER</span>  *[2026-02-19 17:17:56]*

<div style="border-left: 4px solid #2196F3; padding-left: 12px; margin: 4px 0;">

Fix 1 issue in `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/app/api/teams/[id]/route.ts`:  

**Issue SR-002**: The DELETE handler (starting at line 66) uses `checkTeamAccess()` for authorization. But `checkTeamAccess()` was designed for resource access (read/write) and allows ANY team member. This means any agent that is a member of a closed team can delete it, bypassing governance. Team deletion of a closed team should require MANAGER or Chief-of-Staff authority.  

**Fix**: After the existing `checkTeamAccess` check, add an additional authorization check for closed teams:  

1. The file already imports `getTeam` and `getManagerId` from the right places (line 2-3)  
2. Also import `isManager` from `@/lib/governance` — add it to the existing import from governance on line 3  
3. After the `checkTeamAccess` check (line 74-77), add:  
   ```typescript
   // SR-002 fix: Closed team deletion requires elevated authority (MANAGER or COS)
   // checkTeamAccess allows any member for resource access, but deletion is destructive
   const team = getTeam(id)
   if (team && team.type === 'closed') {
     if (agentId && !isManager(agentId) && team.chiefOfStaffId !== agentId) {
       return NextResponse.json(
         { error: 'Closed team deletion requires MANAGER or Chief-of-Staff authority' },
         { status: 403 }
       )
     }
   }
   ```
4. The `agentId` check (`if (agentId && ...`) allows web UI requests (agentId=undefined) to still delete — this is consistent with Phase 1 design where web UI is the admin interface.  

This is a minimal change that adds the governance guard without changing the existing ACL system.  

REPORTING RULES:  
- Write ALL detailed output to a timestamped .md file in docs_dev/ (or scripts_dev/ for scripts)  
- Return to orchestrator ONLY: "[DONE/FAILED] <task> - <one-line result>. Report: <filepath>"  
- NEVER return code blocks, file contents, long lists, or verbose explanations to orchestrator  
- Max 2 lines of text back to orchestrator  

</div>
